<rating>1</rating>< Review>
Please read my honest review, the other reviews are left by employees and family members. I wish i would have had a real review before I went there. I am a mid-thirties, educated, white male executive currently with my wife expecting our first child. I live in the Tujunga area and frequent restaurants often. I have NEVER written a poor review. This place deserves one. My wife is pregnant and craving tacos, so we looked up near by areas and found this place. We looked at THEIR WEBSITE to check out the prices. They seemed reasonable. $1.25 per taco, you choose any meat. When I got to the restaurant I ordered 10 tacos.  she gave me a total of 17.50. I asked how can that be. She explained that the tacos are $1.75. I thought no big deal, I'd buy them any because my wife really wanted tacos. Well I reached in my pocket and realized I left my wallet on the counter. I had $15 in cash on me. I never carry very much cash. This amount would have been fine if the prices of the tacos were priced the same as the website. I kindly showed her the website prices. She said she could not price match. But these were their prices they had listed! She rudely refused, as if I was trying to swindle her. I wasn't. I was prepared to pay the price they advertised. I didn't want to inconvenience them but I asked to give her $15 in exchange for the 10 tacos.  This was only $2.50 off due to their pricing error. I am not a bad customer, but I feel they looked at me and  figured I should have the money so they could make up whatever price they like. Even though I do well for myself, I don't like being taken advantage of. Instead of ordering there, I went down the street to El Pollo Loco. I told them what happened and they offered me $5 off their $20 meal. That's customer service. I left them a great review. I didn't want to go to chain restaurant, I wanted to support a small business. But hey, there are plenty of great Mexican food spots in the area. DO NOT go to this one!</Review>

<rate>3< /rate>< text>
The car wash is as good as most automatic washes and thankfully they reclaim their water. Additionally, if you buy the highest level wash they will re wash it within 72 hours at no cost. The one piece of their business that rubbed me wrong was that they advertise that if it rains within 72 hours of your wash they will also re wash it. The problem is that you have to have it re washed within the 72 hours even if it is still raining. To me this means their push to have you get it washed even if it might rain soon is very misleading and now I know not to trust that.<//text>

<response>None< /response>< text>
The price of the carwash isn't too bad $6.95 I paid. But the car wash itself was fairly poor. It didn't do the rims very well and the people who sprayed the pre-wash on didn't really get the whole car so as a result it wasn't very clean when I came out and the air dryer didn't dry the car off very well. On the plus side, the vacume area was nice. Hoses on both sides of your car. Nice long hose length. Detail attachments on the ends. Floormat clip boards for hanging your floormats. Trash cans on both sides. And untimed self vacume ability was included in the price of the carwash. The place was tidy. Garbage cans kept emptied. I found it a bit cramped to drive around at in a larger vehicle but managable.
Its certianly much nicer looking with its modern glass walls letting you view the cars go thru the wash and better equipped vacume wise than the self serve carwash down the block. But if you dont mind doing it yourself and like a little elbow room and a wash that gets off the heavy grime and dont need the entertainment of seeing how a drivethru carwash works then skip going to Splash. It's basicly only good for a quicky exterior wash job and a really good vacume.
But for the price just the untimed vacume is worth going there thats why i gave it a 3 star rating.<//text>
